const XO = "/".replace(/\/$/, "");
async function X(e, t) {
    const n = await fetch(`${XO}/api${e}`, {
        credentials: "include",
        ...t,
        headers: {
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            ...t?.headers ?? {}
        }
    });
    if (!n.ok) {
        const r = await n.json().catch( () => ({
            error: n.statusText
        }));
        throw new Error(r?.error ?? n.statusText)
    }
    return n.json()
}

function px() {
    const [e] = $()
      , [t,n] = l.useState("idle")
      , r = l.useRef(e)
      , o = l.useRef(null)
      , a = l.useRef(null);
    return l.useEffect( () => {
        if (e !== r.current)
            return r.current = e,
            o.current && clearTimeout(o.current),
            a.current && clearTimeout(a.current),
            n("running"),
            o.current = setTimeout( () => {
                n("done"),
                a.current = setTimeout( () => n("idle"), 350)
            }
            , 120),
            () => {
                o.current && clearTimeout(o.current),
                a.current && clearTimeout(a.current)
            }
    }
    , [e]),
    t === "idle" ? null : s.jsx("div", {
        className: "fixed top-0 left-0 right-0 z-[9999] h-[2px] pointer-events-none overflow-hidden",
        children: s.jsx("div", {
            className: "h-full bg-primary shadow-[0_0_8px_1px] shadow-primary/60 transition-all",
            style: {
                width: t === "running" ? "75%" : "100%",
                transitionDuration: t === "running" ? "200ms" : "150ms",
                transitionTimingFunction: t === "running" ? "ease-out" : "ease-in",
                opacity: t === "done" ? 0 : 1,
                transitionProperty: "width, opacity"
            }
        })
    })
}

function ge(e) {
    if (!(e instanceof Error))
        return !1;
    const t = e.message ?? "";
    return t.includes("Failed to fetch dynamically imported module") || t.includes("Importing a module script failed") || t.includes("error loading dynamically imported module") || t.includes("Unable to preload CSS") || /Loading chunk \d+ failed/.test(t)
}
class Cb extends l.Component {
    state = {
        hasError: !1,
        isChunk: !1
    };
    static getDerivedStateFromError(t) {
        return {
            hasError: !0,
            isChunk: ge(t)
        }
    }
    componentDidCatch(t, n) {
        ge(t) ? setTimeout( () => window.location.reload(), 1500) : console.error("[ErrorBoundary] Unhandled render error:", t, n)
    }
    render() {
        return this.state.hasError ? this.state.isChunk ? s.jsx("div", {
            className: "flex min-h-[100dvh] items-center justify-center bg-background text-foreground",
            children: s.jsxs("div", {
                className: "text-center space-y-3 px-4",
                children: [s.jsx("div", {
                    className: "animate-spin w-8 h-8 border-4 border-primary border-t-transparent rounded-full mx-auto"
                }), s.jsx("p", {
                    className: "text-sm text-muted-foreground",
                    children: "Refreshing app…"
                })]
            })
        }) : s.jsx("div", {
            className: "flex min-h-[100dvh] items-center justify-center bg-background text-foreground",
            children: s.jsxs("div", {
                className: "text-center space-y-4 px-6 max-w-sm",
                children: [s.jsx("h2", {
                    className: "text-lg font-semibold",
                    children: "Something went wrong"
                }), s.jsx("p", {
                    className: "text-sm text-muted-foreground",
                    children: "An unexpected error occurred. Refreshing the page usually fixes it."
                }), s.jsx("button", {
                    onClick: () => window.location.reload(),
                    className: "px-4 py-2 text-sm rounded-md bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:opacity-90 transition-opacity",
                    children: "Reload page"
                })]
            })
        }) : this.props.children
    }
}
window.addEventListener("unhandledrejection", e => {
    const t = e.reason;
    t instanceof Error && (t.message.includes("Failed to fetch dynamically imported module") || t.message.includes("Importing a module script failed") || t.message.includes("error loading dynamically imported module") || /Loading chunk \d+ failed/.test(t.message)) && (e.preventDefault(),
    setTimeout( () => window.location.reload(), 1500))
}
);

    children: s.jsx(Rb, {})
}));
